\DoxyCodeLine{3470 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{class} DataType>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3471 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_data_container_aae8cdb2bcc3b900ec22f26df3e7d67c7}{QCPDataContainer<DataType>::preallocateGrow}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} minimumPreallocSize) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (minimumPreallocSize <= mPreallocSize) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3474     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} newPreallocSize = minimumPreallocSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475     newPreallocSize += (1u << qBound(4, mPreallocIteration + 4, 15)) -\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476                        12;  \textcolor{comment}{// do 4 up to 32768-\/12 preallocation, doubling in each intermediate iteration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477     ++mPreallocIteration;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3479     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} sizeDifference = newPreallocSize -\/ mPreallocSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480     mData.resize(mData.size() + sizeDifference);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481     std::copy\_backward(mData.begin() + mPreallocSize, mData.end() -\/ sizeDifference, mData.end());}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482     mPreallocSize = newPreallocSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3499 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{class} DataType>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_data_container_a83c25ac14be1c920df85e797ee75c982}{QCPDataContainer<DataType>::performAutoSqueeze}}() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} totalAlloc = mData.capacity();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} postAllocSize = totalAlloc -\/ mData.size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} usedSize = size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} shrinkPostAllocation = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} shrinkPreAllocation = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (totalAlloc > 650000)  \textcolor{comment}{// if allocation is larger, shrink earlier with respect to total used size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508         shrinkPostAllocation =}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509             postAllocSize >}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510             usedSize * 1.5;  \textcolor{comment}{// QVector grow strategy is 2\string^n for static data. Watch out not to oscillate!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511         shrinkPreAllocation = mPreallocSize * 10 > usedSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (totalAlloc > 1000)  \textcolor{comment}{// below 10 MiB raw data be generous with preallocated memory, below 1k}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513                                    \textcolor{comment}{// points don't even bother}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515         shrinkPostAllocation = postAllocSize > usedSize * 5;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3516         shrinkPreAllocation =}
\DoxyCodeLine{3517             mPreallocSize > usedSize * 1.5;  \textcolor{comment}{// preallocation can grow into postallocation, so can be smaller}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3518     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3519 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3520     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (shrinkPreAllocation || shrinkPostAllocation) squeeze(shrinkPreAllocation, shrinkPostAllocation);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3521 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4256                                            \textcolor{comment}{// function, but checking here is faster, because we have access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4257                                            \textcolor{comment}{// to QCPAbstractItem::selectable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4258             \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4259         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!currentItem-\/>clipToAxisRect() ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4260             currentItem-\/>clipRect().contains(pos.toPoint()))  \textcolor{comment}{// only consider clicks inside axis cliprect of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4261                                                               \textcolor{comment}{// the item if actually clipped to it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4262         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4263             \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} currentDistance = currentItem-\/>selectTest(pos, \textcolor{keyword}{false});}

\DoxyCodeLine{4267             \}}
